cd newpolka/tests/libFuzzer; \
    number=0 ; while [ ${number} -le 5 ] ; do \
	clang -lstdc++ -fsanitize-coverage=trace-pc-guard -I /usr/local/include -L /home/apron/itv/ -L /home/apron/apron/ -L /home/apron/newpolka/ test_poly.c test_poly${number}.c \
		  /home/libFuzzer.a -o test${number} -lmpfr -lgmp -lapron -litv -lpolkaRll; \
        startTime=`date +%s` ; \
	./test${number} -max_len=10000 -detect_leaks=0 -rss_limit_mb=0 -max_total_time=3600 -print_final_stats=1 MY_CORPUS/ SEED_CORPUS/; \
        endTime=`date +%s` ; \
        runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
        echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_poly$number\n" ; \
	number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true

	clang -lstdc++ -fsanitize-coverage=trace-pc-guard -I /usr/local/include -L /home/apron/itv/ -L /home/apron/apron/ -L /home/apron/newpolka/ test_poly.c test_poly${number}.c \

        startTime=`date +%s` ; \
	./test${number} -max_len=10000 -detect_leaks=0 -rss_limit_mb=0 -max_total_time=3600 -print_final_stats=1 MY_CORPUS/ SEED_CORPUS/; \

        runtime=`expr $endTime - $startTime` ; \
        echo "Execution time: $runtime sec for test_poly$number\n" ; \
	number=`expr $number + 1` ; \
    	done; \
        true
